< Review>
This food is fantastic. However, for a primarily To-Go business, their containers are cheap and flimsy. I wanted to suggest upgrading that for your customers. Unfortunately I came on a day that you were also out of bags. So my ceviche crunch got all over me and my car. I ended up throwing it away and consider it a complete waste. Ceviche has a lot of juice to it which doesn't hold well in a large square container. I'd like to finish by saying the food is fantastic when you get to eat it.</Review>

I had the wonderful experience of trying Sinaloense while visiting from Chicago. We had their steak & barbacoa tacos along with their "Ceviche Crunch." I loved it so much I came back with a bunch of my family also visiting from Texas a few days later. <Rating>2<//Rating>< review>
Food is good, service is awkward and lack-luster.

I came here with my family on a busy weekend to find them understaffed. The hostess (I'm being generous with the term), was uninterested in taking orders and serving customers. At one point the cook was refilling drinks and helping clear customer lines.

We saw plenty of people walk away at the sight of the wait (which wasn't a lot of people), but mostly because the line was stagnant for long periods.

Additionally, a lot of the non-food items are of poor quality. The utensils, for example, may as well have been made of wet noodles.

I'm not sure what happened here, but I don't think I'll be returning.< /review>

< userid>
108950768794183869338< /userid>
<user_name>Daniel Will-Harris</user_name><time>1575012523695< /time><Rating>5</Rating>< text>
Imagine the perfect little country market, if the "country" was the Malibu or Hamptons, and you have Jayde's. Only the best for Bel Air.

The staff is also super friendly, and they stock items you wouldn't expect in a small market, like a staggering selection of wines and spirits. And CBD-infused drinks, chocolates, gummy bears!

Yes, this beautiful little market has the staples: milk, bread, meat, produce. But they're not just any old staples, they are the best, local, organic, fresh and a selection of wines sometimes not available retail elsewhere.

Wolfgang, the on-staff chef, makes sure that everything in the deli is delish. (I don't normally use the word "Delish" but it just seemed fitting). Joe, the manager, is available in case you're looking for something special, and their wine manager will even research and find rare bottles for you.

The fresh house-made soups are fantastic--I've had the sunchoke and the chicken and both are high-end restaurant-worthy.

The butternut squash salad and superb. Even things I don't normally care for, like sausages (house made!) and poke surprised me with their deliciousity.

The Intelligentsia coffee and local pastries are superb! I normally don't like pumpkin lattes, they can just be sweet. Here it was actually savory (with a little sweet). The pastries are baked local and fresh every day. SO much better than the nearby Starbucks.

If you're lucky, you may even see a celebrity there, like Sylvester Stallone or Rod Stewart (I've seen 'em!).

Jayde's is the best!< /text>

I first tasted C√¥te du Rh√¥ne style wine in France in the Rh√¥ne Valley when I was a student. When that winery closed down and I moved to Livermore, I was of course searching for a similar style wine and couldn't find it anywhere except at WOOD Family Vineyards. <rate>5</rate><Review>Best experience with an Optometrist. Saved a trip to the Ophthalmologist thanks to his advanced knowledge of the eye, exam, and the time and patience taken to really check carefully. The only real issues I experienced had to do with insurance and whether vision or medical would cover my prescription lenses and frames; as a result I never did get my sunglasses. So I hope I win the drawing! The staff was always very nice and printed whatever copies I needed. I also had children's eye exams here. I may like a referral to a good vision exercise specialist, but Dr. Ho was able to explain what activities would help develop and maintain good vision, when asked. He's very busy, but good, pointed questions well delivered get quality knowledge back. The waiting area is very nice& modern. The selection of glasses in stock and on order is good. Contacts as well. They even carried the kids sport goggles for athletic activities! Kids option for flip up shaded glasses, and colorful styles, simple lines in basic black, or barely there wire. Also I believe the flex frames. For sunglasses they do carry on order all Transitions lines that have been out. The office is very professional and you can pick up your script or order from their vast stock (most do) keeping a copy for reference. Also, the inventory and insurance runs the range from basic coverage ins stock to very stylish designer brands, purchase with private insurance, cc, cash, or finance. The staff is very helpful in that they generally know what your insurance will cover. There are cash retail options above that and/or add on options. The add on items sometimes make a world of difference in vision clarity and life of lenses.< /Review>< Pictures>

I started with them when I was visiting my mom in Phoenix and decided to sign her and myself up for the year.  We both could really use it since I was told from my PM and PT that massage once a week is best but once a month is good to, I have a bad neck and shoulder. I've stuck with the same person and it works for me.  You need to make sure that you are specific on what you want and going to the same person helps them get familiar with you.  since i have gone i get no more bulging discs in my shoulder because she worked really hard.  her name was Tiffany and thought she was great. < Review>
We had a good experience when we bought our pre-owned 2012 Honda Civic in 2015. Sales staff were professional. However, starting in the winter of 2018, white spots began appearing on our black paint. We didn't think much of it. Then, the paint began to peel off. We discovered that there was an extended warranty for paint issues for Honda Civics, 2012. However, by the time we went to an auto shop and discovered this service bulletin, we were past warranty. Honda corporate has refused to cover our paint job. Now, of course one could argue that we should have done our due diligence or "buyer beware". Fair. I do remember reading about paint issues with Civics before 2010. I assumed that Honda must have fixed the issue. Not true. In fact, do a quick Google search and you'll find people are still having issues with 2020 Honda models and having issues with Honda covering their peeling paint. Before I bought the car, I researched recalls. I didn't realize there was such a thing as a Service Bulletin, which the dealer is not required to tell the buyer about. Now, this bulletin would have gone out to the previous owner, or the dealer before I bought the car. While Clawson was not required to tell me about it, it would have been nice to know that my car may experience peeling paint, what the warning signs are, and that there is an extended warranty for paint on my model. This is clearly a known manufacturing issue Honda should take responsibility for. Paint doesn't just come off a car like this. It looks like a T-Rex scratched our roof. We've gone through all the proper channels to get this covered (through the dealer in our new area) and have been rejected. So, buyer beware.<//Review>

I had a disappointing purchase experience with Clawson Honda. My sales person, Patrick, was fantastic and did his job very well. My issue, and this should come as no surprise to the financing department, was the after-care of my purchase. < review>
7/9/19 Update:

I spoke with Matt and he provided his apologies for the negative customer experience.  We discussed how to correct the issue and he was more than helpful, having his scheduler contact me to set an appointment for the acid wash.  Additionally, he provided me with weather tech floor mats.  This was neither asked nor requested...it was just his kind gesture to correct the wrong.

I have since received the acid wash, the new floor mats, and received a tutorial on all the buttons.  The car LOOKS AMAZING!!!

Though the entire ordeal was not a great experience, the care from management to make things right proved to be awesome.  Hope my post will help others.
--------------------------------------------------------
The process of completing an application online was very easy.  This took a lot of time away from being inside the dealership and alleviated the back and forth banter.  The employees were nice and friendly.  Lastly, Clawson Honda had the best deal for leasing a Civic Hatchback in comparison to Honda North --> ZERO DOWN, ZERO DUE, ZERO SECURITY DEPOSIT, ZERO FIRST MONTH PAYMENT

The reasons that impacted the ratings are:

1. The salesman appeared frustrated when we did not want to commit to the terms of the vehicle on our first visit.  This was visible by his facial expressions and moments when he would "sigh" out of frustration.  As consumers, the salesman needs to cater to our needs and be mindful of these momentary actions.

2. The salesman gave us an incorrect quote on a vehicle.  He stated we would be able to get a Honda Civic Sedan Sport for a cheaper price ($259) than the Honda Civic Hatchback Sport ($269), only to find out it could not happen.  We are happy with the Hatchback but the initial statement was misleading and gave false hopes.  The salesman apologized for this error but our experience had already been negatively impacted.

3.  I just checked the website today (6/7/19) and saw that the Civic Sedan is now available for a cheaper price than the Civic Hatchback.  Salesmen need to have insights into future promotions...I mean only 2 days have elapsed and the car we initially wanted is now being promoted online.  We could have waited!

4. I was told it would only take approximately 20 minutes to sign the appropriate documents and drive off with the vehicle since I was approved for the loan during the online application.  It actually took 1.5 hours.  Because of the long wait time, we did not have time for the salesman to configure our phone/Bluetooth to the system. We will need to come back causing an inconvenience.

5.  In preparation for a vehicle pickup, the car should be prepped, cleaned / washed, and good to go upon completing the signatures.  We had to wait 30 minutes for the car to be washed. The car wash did not remove all the water spots and we are now going to have to come back for an acid wash.  This again will require more efforts on our end.

I hope my experiences will help others.

----------------------------------------------------------------------------
6/11/19 Update: I was informed to contact Matt Roberts to discuss my issues.  I left a voice message and texted him my concerns on Friday 6/7/19.....still no response...If the consumer is truly important, then make it a point to satisfy them.

Also, I completed a Honda Survey and was dumbfounded when it asked if I received a personalized checklist of all items that the salesman should explain and mark off as discussed for a new vehicle.  This was not discussed at all and is very disappointing because they are not following their process.

I lowered my ratings from a 3 star to a 2 star now because of these two additional points.  Clawson still has a great leasing program but needs work on following their processes, employee honesty & knowledge, being empathetic to the customer experience, and going the extra mile to gain the customers' trust and future business.

And I'm still waiting for a response from the Director of Relations.< /review>

< text>
So for starters, I do not have any type of social media nor make any type of reviews, ever! I use Yelp on a daily basis and even then have never wrote a review. I just feel like my experience was so pleasant that I want to share it with future consumers.

Sales guy: Charvon Srey. Young,  funny, professional, informative and attentive. I straight up told him from the beginning what my intentions were. And that was to just take a look at my trading options. I wasn't even serious about purchasing a new vehicle as I already had a brand new 2016 HRV that I enjoyed. Even knowing this his professionalism and kindness did not waver. He continued to ask questions about what I wanted, what I expected, etc.

Although I wasn't rude, I made it very aware that I was ONLY interested in a 2017 Honda CR-V EX AWD and that I did not want to be convinced to upgrade, etc. I also sternly made him aware that I had a very strict payment limit and that I was not willing to budge whatsoever. His answer to that was "Of course, we're going to try our best to give you what you want within the parameters that you've set."

Long story short, after about 2 hours, I walked out of the dealership without the car. The payment did not meet my limit. Like I said, I was not in a desperate situation for a car. Even after two hours of his time and telling him "no" he continued his professionalism and kindness. He even walked me to my car!

We continued to communicate about the car the very next day. Ryan ( amazing number cruncher!) worked some magic and offered a deal and interest rate a lot closer to what I was expecting. Like seriously, they were approximately $50 above my limit. Like a jackhole, I continued to refuse to budge. Charvon did not push.  While at work I kept thinking about it all day and finally I came to the conclusion that the service and professionalism  provided to me, even with my crazy demands and slightly unrealistic expectations of a payment, was invaluable. Any other salesman and finance manager would have heard my intentions and demands and told me to kick rocks. Charvon did not.

So I purchased the vehicle! Yay me! I LOVE it.

Also, to show the extent of Charvon's professionalism and friendliness- I came to the dealership at 5:20PM to sign the papers and told him I needed to be out by 6PM. I know, I'm a total jackhole for expecting the trade in and car buying experience to end in 40minutes. I've had three brand new cars in two years and should have known that it was a super unrealistic expectation. You know what Charvon said? He straight up told me that though he doesn't think that will be the case, he's going to try everything possible to make it happen. It didn't happen. BUT, he tried his very best and I could tell.

I left the dealership at 8PM! Charvon helped me transferred my "garbage" from my HRV to my new CR-V. Poor guy. When he walked up to help me I opened my trunk and I can just see in his face like "Holy bejesus." It was a hot mess. Again, even after he's made the sale, he continued to be ever so helpful. He politely helped me transfer my items, looked under all of my seats for anything i may be missing. He even looked through some of the trash and had me confirm if I wanted them. Such a sweet guy and awesome salesman!

This is my first review ever and as far as I can tell, it's a lot longer than most...oh well. I had to share my awesome experience.

Thanks Clawson Honda!< /text>
